name:Mâ€eâ€iâ€mâ€iâ€aâ€oâ€câ€uâ€iâ€câ€uâ€iâ€sâ€hâ€a

rating:2.5
posted:Posted February 26, 2024
msg:I stayed here on the sixth day of the ***** New Year and had a good experience in the first two days. Although the executive lounge has been moved to the first floor, it is quite rich in content. The hotel also cooperates with Starbucks to produce good coffee. In addition, the hotel also gave away special bookmarks, which are very beautiful and I like them very much.
The biggest displeasure was that on the day of check-out, I ordered a meal in the room at around 2:15. I was told that I would have to wait for 45 minutes, but it was not until 3:10 that all the meals were delivered to the room. It is worth mentioning that the menu is extensive, but the quality of the dishes is disappointing. First, I ordered two cakes. When they arrived, they were both hard and full of ice shards. Another order of Indonesian fried rice, the chicken in it was cooked except for the skin, and the chicken inside was completely raw. Because we were in a hurry to catch a flight, we reported that the chicken was undercooked when we checked out. The lobby first asked us to wait for the Western restaurant manager. Later, the lobby and the manager on duty that day came to add wx separately and said they would communicate with us later. However, the follow-up communication was not to compensate us for our consumption, but to falsely say that we could contact them next time we come to Taiyuan to stay at the Sheraton.
Later, I made a complaint through Taiyuan 12345. First, the marketing person in charge of the Xiaodian District called to understand the situation, and then finally received a call from the manager of the Sheraton Western Restaurant. The other party said that the refund would be received in 2-5 working days, and now it has been It's been a week and I still haven't received my refund. (12345 have already made return visits, and I would like to thank the Taiyuan Municipal Government)
In fact, as a new hotel, Taiyuan Sheraton is remarkable in many aspects, but communication in this hotel is really difficult. Add this and that wx, but none of them can solve the problem. With this Tai Chi service, who would dare to come here a second time?
